<script>
  	options.currentPage = '1';
  	options.totalPages	= '1';
  	options.numberOfPages = '100';
  	options.numberOfPagesArr = [30,50,100,300];
	options.goOffPage = true;
  	var totalSize = '82';

	if(parseInt(totalSize,10) > 0){
		options.onPageClicked = function(event, originalEvent, type, page){
			$('#loading').modal('show');
			//为了控制显示的页数和每页数据多少条增加此参数
			var pageNum = '100';
			var url = "package/list.htm?pageNo="+page+"&pageSize="+pageNum+"&shopId=-1&state=shipped&authId=-1&country=&platform=&isSearch=1&startTime=2016-10-13&endTime=2016-10-13&orderField=shipped_time&isVoided=0&ruleId=-1&sysRule=&isStock=&applyType=&applyStatus=&printJh=-1&printMd=-1&commitPlatform=&productStatus=&jhComment=-1&storageId=0";
			$.ajax({
				type: "GET",
				url: url,
				data: {},
				dataType: "html",
				success: function(data){
					$('#dxmBody').html(data);
					$('#loading').modal('hide');
				}
			});
			$("#keepState").data("ajaxurl",url);
			$("#keepState").data("pagesize",pageNum);
		};

		options.onPageSelected =  function (event){
		   $('#loading').modal('show');
		   var pageSelect =  $(event.target),
			   url = "package/list.htm?pageNo=1&pageSize="+pageSelect.val()+"&shopId=-1&state=shipped&authId=-1&country=&platform=&&isSearch=1&startTime=2016-10-13&endTime=2016-10-13&orderField=shipped_time&isVoided=0&ruleId=-1&sysRule=&applyType=&applyStatus=&printJh=-1&printMd=-1&commitPlatform=&productStatus=&jhComment=-1&storageId=0";
			$.ajax({
				type: "GET",
				url: url,
				data: {},
				dataType: "html",
				success: function(data){
					$('#dxmBody').html(data);
					$('#loading').modal('hide');
				}
			});
			$("#keepState").data("ajaxurl",url);
			$("#keepState").data("pagesize",pageSelect.val());
		};

		options.onPageJump =  function (event){
			$('#loading').modal('show');
			var pageJump =  $(event.target);

			var pageNo = pageJump.prevAll("input[zdyPageInput='zdy']").val();
			var pageSize = $("select[name='pageselct']").val();
			var url = "package/list.htm?pageNo="+pageNo+"&pageSize="+pageSize+"&shopId=-1&state=shipped&authId=-1&country=&platform=&isSearch=1&startTime=2016-10-13&endTime=2016-10-13&orderField=shipped_time&isVoided=0&ruleId=-1&sysRule=&isStock=&applyType=&applyStatus=&printJh=-1&printMd=-1&commitPlatform=&productStatus=&jhComment=-1&storageId=0";

			$.ajax({
				type: "GET",
				url: url,
				data: {},
				dataType: "html",
				success: function(data){
					$('#dxmBody').html(data);
					$('#loading').modal('hide');
				}
			});
			$("#keepState").data("ajaxurl",url);
			$("#keepState").data("pagesize",pageSize);
		};
		$('#upPage').bootstrapPaginator(options);
		$('#downPage').bootstrapPaginator(options);

	} else {
		$('#upPage').empty();
		$('#downPage').empty();
	}
  	
  	// 当前显示的是哪个状态(未处理、异常订单、待发货等)
 	var seledStateName = $("#keepState").data("stateName");
  	$("#currState").html(seledStateName);
  	
  	$(function(){
  		 $("div.listImgIn").picZoom({
  			 imgWidth: "296",
  			 imgHeight: "296",
  		     divWidth: "300",
  		     divHeight:"300"
  		 });
  	});
</script>
